## 第三十章 数据沙箱与测试

### 30.1 功能定位

数据沙箱与测试模块提供隔离的数据测试环境，支持数据使用前的安全验证和分析。该模块帮助用户在不影响生产环境的情况下，安全地探索数据、测试脚本和验证脱敏规则。

核心目标：
1. **环境隔离**：提供与生产环境完全隔离的测试环境
2. **数据脱敏**：在沙箱中对敏感数据进行脱敏验证
3. **安全测试**：允许执行SQL和分析脚本，验证结果准确性
4. **风险控制**：确保沙箱操作不会影响生产数据

### 30.2 沙箱环境创建

#### 30.2.1 环境管理框架

```python
class DataSandboxManager:
    """数据沙箱管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.environment_builder = SandboxEnvironmentBuilder()
        self.data_sampler = DataSampler()
        self.access_controller = SandboxAccessController()
    
    def create_sandbox(self, request: SandboxRequest) -> Sandbox:
        """
        创建数据沙箱
        """
        
        # 1. 验证请求
        validation = self.validate_request(request)
        if not validation.is_valid:
            raise InvalidRequestError(validation.errors)
        
        # 2. 检查资源配额
        quota_check = self.check_resource_quota(request.owner)
        if not quota_check.has_available:
            raise QuotaExceededError(quota_check.message)
        
        # 3. 创建沙箱环境
        sandbox = Sandbox(
            id=self.generate_sandbox_id(),
            name=request.name,
            description=request.description,
            owner=request.owner,
            source_assets=request.source_assets,
            data_sample_rate=request.sample_rate,
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            expires_at=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=request.retention_days),
            status='provisioning'
        )
        
        # 4. 准备样本数据
        sample_data = self.prepare_sample_data(
            source_assets=request.source_assets,
            sample_rate=request.sample_rate,
            anonymization_rules=request.anonymization_rules
        )
        
        # 5. 部署沙箱环境
        self.environment_builder.deploy(
            sandbox_id=sandbox.id,
            data=sample_data,
            compute_resources=request.compute_resources
        )
        
        # 6. 配置访问控制
        self.access_controller.configure(
            sandbox_id=sandbox.id,
            allowed_users=[request.owner] + request.collaborators,
            allowed_operations=request.allowed_operations
        )
        
        sandbox.status = 'ready'
        return sandbox
    
    def prepare_sample_data(self, source_assets: List[AssetReference],
                             sample_rate: float,
                             anonymization_rules: List[Rule]) -> SampleData:
        """
        准备样本数据
        """
        
        sample_result = {}
        
        for asset_ref in source_assets:
            # 1. 获取原始数据
            original_data = self.fetch_source_data(asset_ref)
            
            # 2. 执行采样
            sampled_data = self.data_sampler.sample(
                data=original_data,
                rate=sample_rate,
                method=self.select_sample_method(asset_ref)
            )
            
            # 3. 应用脱敏规则
            if anonymization_rules:
                anonymized_data = self.apply_anonymization(
                    data=sampled_data,
                    rules=anonymization_rules
                )
            else:
                anonymized_data = sampled_data
            
            sample_result[asset_ref.asset_id] = anonymized_data
        
        return SampleData(assets=sample_result)
```

### 30.3 数据脱敏测试

#### 30.3.1 脱敏规则验证

```python
class DesensitizationTester:
    """脱敏测试器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.rule_validator = DesensitizationRuleValidator()
        self.sample_generator = TestSampleGenerator()
        self.impact_analyzer = PrivacyImpactAnalyzer()
    
    def test_desensitization_rules(self, 
                                    rules: List[DesensitizationRule],
                                    test_data: TestDataSet) -> TestResult:
        """
        测试脱敏规则有效性
        """
        
        results = []
        
        for rule in rules:
            # 1. 验证规则语法
            syntax_check = self.rule_validator.check_syntax(rule)
            
            # 2. 执行规则测试
            test_samples = self.sample_generator.generate(
                count=100,
                pattern=rule.target_pattern
            )
            
            test_results = []
            for sample in test_samples:
                original_value = sample.value
                masked_value = rule.apply(sample.value)
                
                test_results.append(SampleTestResult(
                    original=original_value,
                    masked=masked_value,
                    re_identifiable=self.check_re_identification(masked_value)
                ))
            
            # 3. 分析隐私影响
            impact = self.impact_analyzer.analyze(
                rule=rule,
                test_results=test_results
            )
            
            # 4. 生成测试报告
            results.append(DesensitizationTestResult(
                rule_id=rule.id,
                rule_name=rule.name,
                syntax_valid=syntax_check.is_valid,
                syntax_errors=syntax_check.errors,
                test_count=len(test_results),
                success_count=sum(1 for r in test_results if not r.re_identifiable),
                privacy_impact=impact
            ))
        
        return TestResult(
            overall_pass=all(r.success_count > 0 for r in results),
            results=results
        )
    
    def validate_production_rules(self, 
                                   rules: List[DesensitizationRule]) -> ValidationReport:
        """
        验证生产脱敏规则
        """
        
        # 1. 单元测试
        unit_results = self.run_unit_tests(rules)
        
        # 2. 集成测试
        integration_results = self.run_integration_tests(rules)
        
        # 3. 性能测试
        performance_results = self.run_performance_tests(rules)
        
        # 4. 合规性检查
        compliance_results = self.check_compliance(rules)
        
        return ValidationReport(
            unit_tests=unit_results,
            integration_tests=integration_results,
            performance_tests=performance_results,
            compliance_checks=compliance_results,
            overall_valid=all([
                unit_results.passed,
                integration_results.passed,
                performance_results.passed,
                compliance_results.passed
            ])
        )
```

### 30.4 分析脚本测试

#### 30.4.1 安全执行环境

```python
class ScriptTestingEngine:
    """脚本测试引擎"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.sandbox_executor = SandboxExecutor()
        self.result_comparator = ResultComparator()
        self.impact_monitor = ImpactMonitor()
    
    def test_script(self, 
                    script: AnalysisScript,
                    sandbox_id: str,
                    production_baseline: bool = True) -> TestReport:
        """
        在沙箱中测试分析脚本
        """
        
        # 1. 获取生产基线结果（如需要）
        baseline_result = None
        if production_baseline:
            baseline_result = self.get_baseline_result(script)
        
        # 2. 在沙箱中执行脚本
        sandbox_result = self.sandbox_executor.execute(
            sandbox_id=sandbox_id,
            script=script,
            timeout_seconds=script.timeout or 300
        )
        
        # 3. 对比结果
        comparison = None
        if baseline_result:
            comparison = self.result_comparator.compare(
                baseline=baseline_result,
                sandbox=sandbox_result,
                tolerance=script.result_tolerance
            )
        
        # 4. 监控资源使用
        resource_usage = self.impact_monitor.get_usage(sandbox_id)
        
        # 5. 生成测试报告
        return TestReport(
            script_id=script.id,
            script_name=script.name,
            execution_time=sandbox_result.execution_time,
            result_count=sandbox_result.row_count,
            baseline_available=baseline_result is not None,
            result_match=comparison.is_match if comparison else None,
            difference_details=comparison.details if comparison else None,
            resource_usage=resource_usage,
            warnings=sandbox_result.warnings,
            status='passed' if self.is_acceptable(sandbox_result, comparison) else 'failed'
        )
```

### 30.5 沙箱隔离保障

#### 30.5.1 隔离机制实现

```python
class SandboxIsolationManager:
    """沙箱隔离管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.network_isolator = NetworkIsolator()
        self.compute_quota = ComputeQuotaManager()
        self.data_firewall = DataFirewall()
        self.audit_logger = SandboxAuditLogger()
    
    def verify_isolation(self, sandbox_id: str) -> IsolationVerification:
        """
        验证沙箱隔离性
        """
        
        checks = []
        
        # 1. 网络隔离检查
        network_check = self.network_isolator.verify(
            sandbox_id=sandbox_id,
            allowed_destinations=['sandbox-storage'],
            blocked_destinations=['production-db', 'external-api']
        )
        checks.append(('network', network_check))
        
        # 2. 计算配额检查
        quota_check = self.compute_quota.verify(
            sandbox_id=sandbox_id,
            limits={
                'cpu': '4 cores',
                'memory': '16GB',
                'disk_io': '100MB/s',
                'network_bandwidth': '10Mbps'
            }
        )
        checks.append(('compute_quota', quota_check))
        
        # 3. 数据防火墙检查
        firewall_check = self.data_firewall.verify(
            sandbox_id=sandbox_id,
            blocked_operations=['TRUNCATE', 'DROP', 'DELETE without WHERE']
        )
        checks.append(('data_firewall', firewall_check))
        
        # 4. 审计日志检查
        audit_check = self.audit_logger.verify(
            sandbox_id=sandbox_id,
            required_logging=['SELECT', 'script_execution', 'data_export']
        )
        checks.append(('audit', audit_check))
        
        return IsolationVerification(
            sandbox_id=sandbox_id,
            checks=checks,
            is_isolated=all(c[1].passed for c in checks),
            verified_at=datetime.now()
        )
```

## 第三十一章 数据版本管理

### 31.1 功能定位

数据版本管理模块提供数据表结构、模型、脚本等资产的版本化管理能力，支持版本历史查看、版本对比和变更回滚。

核心目标：
1. **变更追踪**：完整记录资产的变更历史
2. **版本对比**：支持任意两个版本之间的差异对比
3. **安全回滚**：支持将资产回滚到指定的历史版本
4. **协作管理**：支持分支开发和版本合并

### 31.2 表结构版本

#### 31.2.1 版本追踪机制

```python
class SchemaVersionManager:
    """表结构版本管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.version_repository = VersionRepository()
        self.diff_generator = SchemaDiffGenerator()
        self.rollback_engine = RollbackEngine()
    
    def record_change(self, asset_id: str, 
                      new_schema: SchemaDefinition,
                      change_type: str,
                      changed_by: str) -> SchemaVersion:
        """
        记录表结构变更
        """
        
        # 1. 获取当前版本
        current_version = self.version_repository.get_latest(asset_id)
        
        # 2. 生成变更差异
        diff = self.diff_generator.generate(
            old_schema=current_version.schema if current_version else None,
            new_schema=new_schema
        )
        
        # 3. 创建新版本
        new_version = SchemaVersion(
            id=self.generate_version_id(),
            asset_id=asset_id,
            version_number=self.increment_version(current_version),
            schema=new_schema,
            diff=diff,
            change_type=change_type,
            changed_by=changed_by,
            changed_at=datetime.now(),
            change_reason=None  # 可要求填写
        )
        
        # 4. 保存版本
        return self.version_repository.save(new_version)
    
    def get_version_history(self, asset_id: str,
                            limit: int = 50) -> List[SchemaVersion]:
        """
        获取版本历史
        """
        
        versions = self.version_repository.get_history(
            asset_id=asset_id,
            limit=limit
        )
        
        return sorted(versions, key=lambda v: v.version_number, reverse=True)
    
    def compare_versions(self, asset_id: str,
                        version_a: int,
                        version_b: int) -> VersionComparison:
        """
        对比两个版本
        """
        
        v_a = self.version_repository.get_version(asset_id, version_a)
        v_b = self.version_repository.get_version(asset_id, version_b)
        
        return VersionComparison(
            version_a=v_a,
            version_b=v_b,
            diff=self.diff_generator.generate(v_a.schema, v_b.schema),
            added_fields=self.diff_generator.get_added_fields(),
            removed_fields=self.diff_generator.get_removed_fields(),
            modified_fields=self.diff_generator.get_modified_fields()
        )
    
    def rollback_to_version(self, asset_id: str,
                           target_version: int,
                           reason: str) -> RollbackResult:
        """
        回滚到指定版本
        """
        
        # 1. 验证回滚可行性
        feasibility = self.rollback_engine.check_feasibility(
            asset_id=asset_id,
            target_version=target_version
        )
        
        if not feasibility.can_rollback:
            raise RollbackNotAllowedError(feasibility.reasons)
        
        # 2. 创建备份
        backup = self.create_backup(asset_id)
        
        # 3. 执行回滚
        result = self.rollback_engine.execute(
            asset_id=asset_id,
            target_version=target_version,
            backup=backup,
            reason=reason
        )
        
        return result
```

### 31.3 模型版本管理

#### 31.3.1 版本分支机制

```python
class ModelVersionManager:
    """数据模型版本管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.branch_manager = BranchManager()
        self.merge_engine = MergeEngine()
        self.conflict_resolver = ConflictResolver()
    
    def create_branch(self, 
                      source_asset_id: str,
                      branch_name: str,
                      created_by: str) -> ModelBranch:
        """
        创建模型分支
        """
        
        # 1. 获取源分支最新版本
        source_version = self.version_repository.get_latest(source_asset_id)
        
        # 2. 创建分支
        branch = ModelBranch(
            id=self.generate_branch_id(),
            name=branch_name,
            asset_id=source_asset_id,
            base_version=source_version.version_number,
            created_by=created_by,
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            status='active'
        )
        
        return self.branch_manager.create(branch)
    
    def commit_changes(self, 
                      branch_id: str,
                      changes: List[ModelChange],
                      message: str) -> CommitResult:
        """
        提交变更到分支
        """
        
        # 1. 创建提交
        commit = ModelCommit(
            id=self.generate_commit_id(),
            branch_id=branch_id,
            message=message,
            changes=changes,
            author=self.get_current_user(),
            committed_at=datetime.now()
        )
        
        # 2. 验证变更
        validation = self.validate_changes(changes)
        if not validation.is_valid:
            raise InvalidChangesError(validation.errors)
        
        # 3. 应用变更
        self.apply_changes(branch_id, changes)
        
        # 4. 保存提交
        return CommitResult(
            commit_id=commit.id,
            branch_id=branch_id,
            changes_applied=len(changes)
        )
    
    def merge_branch(self, 
                    source_branch_id: str,
                    target_branch_id: str) -> MergeResult:
        """
        合并分支
        """
        
        # 1. 获取分支最新提交
        source_commits = self.get_branch_commits(source_branch_id)
        target_commits = self.get_branch_commits(target_branch_id)
        
        # 2. 检测冲突
        conflicts = self.detect_conflicts(source_commits, target_commits)
        
        if conflicts:
            # 3. 解决冲突
            resolution = self.conflict_resolver.resolve(conflicts)
            
            return MergeResult(
                status='conflicts_resolved',
                conflicts=conflicts,
                resolution=resolution
            )
        
        # 4. 执行合并
        merge_result = self.merge_engine.execute(
            source_branch_id=source_branch_id,
            target_branch_id=target_branch_id
        )
        
        return MergeResult(
            status='success',
            merge_commit_id=merge_result.commit_id,
            changes_merged=merge_result.change_count
        )
```

### 31.4 脚本版本管理

#### 31.4.1 代码版本控制

```python
class ScriptVersionControl:
    """脚本版本控制"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.version_store = ScriptVersionStore()
        self.code_reviewer = CodeReviewer()
        self.change_tracker = ChangeTracker()
    
    def save_script_version(self,
                           script_id: str,
                           content: str,
                           metadata: ScriptMetadata) -> ScriptVersion:
        """
        保存脚本版本
        """
        
        # 1. 计算内容哈希
        content_hash = self.calculate_hash(content)
        
        # 2. 检查是否有变更
        latest_version = self.version_store.get_latest(script_id)
        if latest_version and latest_version.content_hash == content_hash:
            return latest_version  # 无变更，直接返回
        
        # 3. 计算变更统计
        change_stats = self.change_tracker.compute_stats(
            old_content=latest_version.content if latest_version else None,
            new_content=content
        )
        
        # 4. 创建新版本
        version = ScriptVersion(
            id=self.generate_version_id(),
            script_id=script_id,
            content=content,
            content_hash=content_hash,
            line_count=len(content.splitlines()),
            change_stats=change_stats,
            author=metadata.author,
            commit_message=metadata.commit_message,
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        
        return self.version_store.save(version)
    
    def create_review_request(self,
                             version_id: str,
                             reviewers: List[str]) -> ReviewRequest:
        """
        创建代码评审请求
        """
        
        version = self.version_store.get(version_id)
        
        review_request = ReviewRequest(
            id=self.generate_review_id(),
            version_id=version_id,
            script_id=version.script_id,
            reviewers=reviewers,
            changes=version.change_stats,
            created_by=version.author,
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            status='pending'
        )
        
        return self.code_reviewer.create_request(review_request)
    
    def get_change_history(self, 
                          script_id: str,
                          since_version: int = None) -> ChangeHistory:
        """
        获取变更历史
        """
        
        versions = self.version_store.get_history(
            script_id=script_id,
            since_version=since_version
        )
        
        return ChangeHistory(
            script_id=script_id,
            versions=versions,
            total_changes=sum(v.change_stats.lines_changed for v in versions),
            contributor_stats=self.compute_contributor_stats(versions)
        )
```

### 31.5 变更通知

#### 31.5.1 订阅通知机制

```python
class VersionChangeNotifier:
    """版本变更通知器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.subscription_manager = SubscriptionManager()
        self.notification_service = NotificationService()
    
    def notify_change(self, 
                     asset_id: str,
                     version: SchemaVersion,
                     subscribers: List[Subscriber]) -> None:
        """
        通知订阅者变更
        """
        
        for subscriber in subscribers:
            # 1. 检查订阅类型
            if not self.should_notify(subscriber, version):
                continue
            
            # 2. 生成通知内容
            notification = self.generate_notification(
                subscriber=subscriber,
                asset_id=asset_id,
                version=version
            )
            
            # 3. 发送通知
            self.notification_service.send(
                user_id=subscriber.user_id,
                notification=notification,
                channels=subscriber.preferred_channels
            )
    
    def generate_notification(self,
                             subscriber: Subscriber,
                             asset_id: str,
                             version: SchemaVersion) -> Notification:
        """
        生成变更通知
        """
        
        asset = self.get_asset(asset_id)
        diff_summary = self.generate_diff_summary(version.diff)
        
        return Notification(
            title=f"【{asset.name}】发生结构变更",
            content=f"""
                版本：v{version.version_number}
                变更类型：{version.change_type}
                变更人：{version.changed_by}
                变更时间：{version.changed_at}
                
                变更摘要：
                {diff_summary}
                
                {self.get_view_url(asset_id, version.version_number)}
            """,
            type='schema_change',
            priority='normal' if version.change_type == 'minor' else 'high',
            action_url=self.get_change_detail_url(asset_id, version.version_number)
        )
```

## 第三十二章 数据资产协作中心

### 32.1 功能定位

数据资产协作中心模块提供围绕数据资产的团队协作和知识沉淀能力，包括评论讨论、问答社区、关注订阅等功能，促进用户之间的知识共享和协作。

核心目标：
1. **知识沉淀**：通过评论和讨论积累数据资产的使用经验
2. **协作问答**：提供问答社区解答用户疑问
3. **关注订阅**：支持用户关注感兴趣的内容并获取更新通知
4. **协作编辑**：支持多人协作编辑资产文档

### 32.2 资产评论

#### 32.2.1 评论系统设计

```python
class AssetCommentSystem:
    """资产评论系统"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.comment_repository = CommentRepository()
        self.user_mention = UserMentionParser()
        self.content_filter = ContentFilter()
        self.notification_service = NotificationService()
    
    def add_comment(self, 
                   asset_id: str,
                   user_id: str,
                   content: str,
                   parent_id: str = None) -> Comment:
        """
        添加评论
        """
        
        # 1. 内容安全检查
        safety_check = self.content_filter.check(content)
        if not safety_check.is_safe:
            raise ContentSafetyError(safety_check.violations)
        
        # 2. 解析@提及
        mentions = self.user_mention.parse(content)
        
        # 3. 创建评论
        comment = Comment(
            id=self.generate_comment_id(),
            asset_id=asset_id,
            user_id=user_id,
            content=content,
            mentions=mentions,
            parent_id=parent_id,
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            status='published'
        )
        
        # 4. 保存评论
        saved_comment = self.comment_repository.save(comment)
        
        # 5. 发送通知
        self.notify_mentions(saved_comment, mentions)
        self.notify_asset_owner(saved_comment)
        
        return saved_comment
    
    def get_asset_comments(self,
                          asset_id: str,
                          page: int = 1,
                          page_size: int = 20) -> PaginatedComments:
        """
        获取资产评论列表
        """
        
        comments = self.comment_repository.get_by_asset(
            asset_id=asset_id,
            page=page,
            page_size=page_size
        )
        
        # 组织评论树结构
        comment_tree = self.organize_as_tree(comments)
        
        return PaginatedComments(
            comments=comment_tree,
            total=len(comments),
            page=page,
            page_size=page_size,
            has_more=(page * page_size) < len(comments)
        )
    
    def resolve_thread(self, thread_id: str, resolved_by: str) -> Thread:
        """
        标记讨论为已解决
        """
        
        thread = self.comment_repository.get_thread(thread_id)
        thread.status = 'resolved'
        thread.resolved_by = resolved_by
        thread.resolved_at = datetime.now()
        
        return self.comment_repository.save(thread)
```

### 32.3 问答社区

#### 32.3.1 问答系统设计

```python
class QACommunitySystem:
    """问答社区系统"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.question_repository = QuestionRepository()
        self.answer_repository = AnswerRepository()
        self.vote_manager = VoteManager()
        self.reputation_tracker = ReputationTracker()
    
    def post_question(self,
                     user_id: str,
                     title: str,
                     content: str,
                     related_assets: List[str],
                     tags: List[str]) -> Question:
        """
        发布问题
        """
        
        # 1. 内容检查
        quality_check = self.check_question_quality(title, content)
        if not quality_check.passes:
            raise LowQualityQuestionError(quality_check.suggestions)
        
        # 2. 创建问题
        question = Question(
            id=self.generate_question_id(),
            user_id=user_id,
            title=title,
            content=content,
            related_assets=related_assets,
            tags=tags,
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            status='open',
            view_count=0,
            vote_count=0,
            answer_count=0
        )
        
        # 3. 保存问题
        return self.question_repository.save(question)
    
    def post_answer(self,
                   question_id: str,
                   user_id: str,
                   content: str) -> Answer:
        """
        发布回答
        """
        
        question = self.question_repository.get(question_id)
        
        # 1. 创建回答
        answer = Answer(
            id=self.generate_answer_id(),
            question_id=question_id,
            user_id=user_id,
            content=content,
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            vote_count=0,
            is_accepted=False
        )
        
        saved_answer = self.answer_repository.save(answer)
        
        # 2. 更新问题统计
        question.answer_count += 1
        self.question_repository.save(question)
        
        # 3. 通知提问者
        self.notify_question_owner(question, saved_answer)
        
        return saved_answer
    
    def accept_answer(self,
                      question_id: str,
                      answer_id: str,
                      accepted_by: str) -> None:
        """
        采纳回答
        """
        
        question = self.question_repository.get(question_id)
        
        # 验证权限
        if question.user_id != accepted_by:
            raise PermissionDeniedError("只有提问者可以采纳回答")
        
        # 取消之前的采纳
        if question.accepted_answer_id:
            previous_answer = self.answer_repository.get(question.accepted_answer_id)
            previous_answer.is_accepted = False
            self.answer_repository.save(previous_answer)
        
        # 采纳新回答
        new_answer = self.answer_repository.get(answer_id)
        new_answer.is_accepted = True
        self.answer_repository.save(new_answer)
        
        # 更新问题
        question.accepted_answer_id = answer_id
        question.status = 'resolved'
        self.question_repository.save(question)
        
        # 增加回答者积分
        self.reputation_tracker.award(
            user_id=new_answer.user_id,
            points=15,  # 采纳答案奖励
            reason='answer_accepted'
        )
    
    def vote(self, 
            content_type: str,  # 'question' or 'answer'
            content_id: str,
            user_id: str,
            vote_type: str) -> VoteResult:  # 'up' or 'down'
        """
        投票
        """
        
        return self.vote_manager.vote(
            content_type=content_type,
            content_id=content_id,
            user_id=user_id,
            vote_type=vote_type
        )
```

### 32.4 关注与订阅

#### 32.4.1 订阅管理

```python
class SubscriptionManager:
    """订阅管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.subscription_repository = SubscriptionRepository()
        self.notification_queue = NotificationQueue()
    
    def subscribe(self,
                 user_id: str,
                 target_type: str,  # 'asset', 'category', 'tag'
                 target_id: str,
                 subscription_type: str) -> Subscription:  # 'all', 'major_only', 'digest'
        """
        订阅内容
        """
        
        # 检查是否已订阅
        existing = self.subscription_repository.find(
            user_id=user_id,
            target_type=target_type,
            target_id=target_id
        )
        
        if existing:
            # 更新订阅类型
            existing.subscription_type = subscription_type
            return self.subscription_repository.save(existing)
        
        # 创建新订阅
        subscription = Subscription(
            id=self.generate_subscription_id(),
            user_id=user_id,
            target_type=target_type,
            target_id=target_id,
            subscription_type=subscription_type,
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            status='active'
        )
        
        return self.subscription_repository.save(subscription)
    
    def notify_subscribers(self,
                          event: ContentEvent) -> None:
        """
        通知订阅者
        """
        
        subscribers = self.subscription_repository.get_subscribers(
            target_type=event.target_type,
            target_id=event.target_id
        )
        
        for subscriber in subscribers:
            # 检查订阅类型匹配
            if not self.matches_subscription_type(subscriber, event):
                continue
            
            # 生成通知
            notification = self.generate_notification(subscriber, event)
            
            # 加入通知队列
            self.notification_queue.enqueue(notification)
    
    def get_user_subscriptions(self,
                               user_id: str,
                               page: int = 1,
                               page_size: int = 20) -> PaginatedSubscriptions:
        """
        获取用户订阅列表
        """
        
        return self.subscription_repository.get_by_user(
            user_id=user_id,
            page=page,
            page_size=page_size
        )
```

### 32.5 协作编辑

#### 32.5.1 协作文档管理

```python
class CollaborativeEditor:
    """协作编辑器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.document_store = DocumentStore()
        self.lock_manager = DocumentLockManager()
        self.change_processor = ChangeProcessor()
        self.version_control = DocumentVersionControl()
    
    def start_editing(self,
                     document_id: str,
                     user_id: str) -> EditSession:
        """
        开始编辑会话
        """
        
        # 1. 获取文档锁
        lock = self.lock_manager.acquire_lock(document_id, user_id)
        
        # 2. 获取文档最新内容
        document = self.document_store.get(document_id)
        
        # 3. 创建编辑会话
        session = EditSession(
            id=self.generate_session_id(),
            document_id=document_id,
            user_id=user_id,
            lock_id=lock.id,
            content=document.content,
            version=document.version,
            started_at=datetime.now()
        )
        
        return session
    
    def apply_changes(self,
                      session_id: str,
                      changes: List[ContentChange]) -> ApplyResult:
        """
        应用变更
        """
        
        session = self.get_session(session_id)
        
        # 1. 验证锁
        if not self.lock_manager.is_valid_lock(session.lock_id):
            raise LockExpiredError()
        
        # 2. 应用变更到本地副本
        new_content = self.change_processor.apply(
            base_content=session.content,
            changes=changes
        )
        
        # 3. 更新会话
        session.content = new_content
        session.pending_changes.extend(changes)
        
        return ApplyResult(
            applied=len(changes),
            current_content=new_content
        )
    
    def save_document(self, session_id: str, commit_message: str) -> DocumentVersion:
        """
        保存文档版本
        """
        
        session = self.get_session(session_id)
        
        # 1. 发布变更
        self.change_processor.publish(session.document_id, session.pending_changes)
        
        # 2. 创建版本
        version = self.version_control.save_version(
            document_id=session.document_id,
            content=session.content,
            changes=session.pending_changes,
            commit_message=commit_message,
            author=session.user_id
        )
        
        # 3. 释放锁
        self.lock_manager.release_lock(session.lock_id)
        
        # 4. 结束会话
        self.end_session(session_id)
        
        return version
```

## 第三十三章 数据安全水印

### 33.1 功能定位

数据安全水印模块提供数据水印嵌入和泄露溯源能力，保护数据资产安全，防止数据泄露和非法传播。

核心目标：
1. **泄露威慑**：通过水印警告潜在的泄露行为
2. **泄露溯源**：当发生泄露时，通过水印追溯泄露源头
3. **证据固化**：为法律诉讼提供不可抵赖的泄露证据
4. **审计追溯**：记录数据导出的完整操作日志

### 33.2 静态水印

#### 33.2.1 水印嵌入机制

```python
class StaticWatermark:
    """静态水印处理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.watermark_generator = WatermarkGenerator()
        self.embedding_engine = WatermarkEmbedder()
        self.verification_tool = WatermarkVerifier()
    
    def embed_watermark(self,
                       data: DataExport,
                       watermark_type: str,
                       config: WatermarkConfig) -> WatermarkedData:
        """
        嵌入静态水印
        """
        
        # 1. 生成水印内容
        watermark_content = self.watermark_generator.generate(
            type=watermark_type,
            user_id=config.user_id,
            export_time=datetime.now(),
            export_id=config.export_id,
            metadata=config.metadata
        )
        
        # 2. 根据数据类型嵌入水印
        if data.type == 'file':
            return self.embed_file_watermark(data, watermark_content, config)
        elif data.type == 'database':
            return self.embed_database_watermark(data, watermark_content, config)
        elif data.type == 'api':
            return self.embed_api_watermark(data, watermark_content, config)
        
        raise UnsupportedDataTypeError(data.type)
    
    def embed_file_watermark(self,
                            data: FileData,
                            watermark: WatermarkContent,
                            config: WatermarkConfig) -> WatermarkedData:
        """
        文件水印嵌入
        """
        
        if config.file_type == 'pdf':
            return self.embed_pdf_watermark(data, watermark, config)
        elif config.file_type in ['xlsx', 'xls']:
            return self.embed_excel_watermark(data, watermark, config)
        elif config.file_type == 'csv':
            return self.embed_csv_watermark(data, watermark, config)
        else:
            return self.embed_generic_file_watermark(data, watermark, config)
    
    def embed_csv_watermark(self,
                           data: FileData,
                           watermark: WatermarkContent,
                           config: WatermarkConfig) -> WatermarkedData:
        """
        CSV文件水印嵌入
        """
        
        content = data.content
        
        # 策略1：追加水印列
        watermark_column = f"_watermark_{watermark.id}"
        watermarked_content = f"{content}\n{watermark_column},\"{watermark.content}\""
        
        # 策略2：嵌入注释行
        watermark_comment = f"# EXPORT_WATERMARK: {watermark.serialize()}"
        
        # 组合使用
        final_content = watermark_comment + "\n" + watermarked_content
        
        return WatermarkedData(
            original=data,
            watermarked_content=final_content,
            watermark=watermark,
            embedding_method='column_and_comment',
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
    
    def embed_pdf_watermark(self,
                           data: FileData,
                           watermark: WatermarkContent,
                           config: WatermarkConfig) -> WatermarkedData:
        """
        PDF文件水印嵌入
        """
        
        # 使用PDF库添加水印
        import pdfplumber
        
        watermark_text = self.format_watermark_text(watermark, config)
        
        with pdfplumber.open(data.path) as pdf:
            # 添加水印到每一页
            for page in pdf.pages:
                page.add_watermark(
                    text=watermark_text,
                    fontname="Helvetica",
                    fontsize=config.font_size or 10,
                    opacity=config.opacity or 0.3,
                    layout=True  # 沿对角线布局
                )
        
        return WatermarkedData(
            original=data,
            watermarked_file=self.save_watermarked_pdf(data),
            watermark=watermark,
            embedding_method='pdf_overlay',
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
```

### 33.3 动态水印

#### 33.3.1 动态水印生成

```python
class DynamicWatermark:
    """动态水印处理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.user_context = UserContextProvider()
        self.renderer = WatermarkRenderer()
        self.token_manager = DynamicTokenManager()
    
    def generate_dynamic_watermark(self,
                                   session_id: str,
                                   target_element: str) -> DynamicWatermarkContent:
        """
        生成动态水印
        """
        
        # 1. 获取当前用户上下文
        user_context = self.user_context.get_context(session_id)
        
        # 2. 生成动态令牌
        token = self.token_manager.generate_token(
            user_id=user_context.user_id,
            session_id=session_id,
            timestamp=datetime.now()
        )
        
        # 3. 构建水印内容
        watermark_content = WatermarkContent(
            user_id=user_context.user_id,
            user_name=user_context.user_name,
            user_email=user_context.email,
            timestamp=datetime.now(),
            session_id=session_id,
            ip_address=user_context.ip_address,
            token=token
        )
        
        # 4. 渲染水印
        rendered = self.renderer.render(
            content=watermark_content,
            style='diagonal',
            opacity=0.2
        )
        
        return DynamicWatermarkContent(
            content=watermark_content,
            rendered=rendered,
            target_element=target_element,
            refresh_interval=300  # 5分钟刷新一次
        )
    
    def apply_to_element(self,
                        element_id: str,
                        watermark: DynamicWatermarkContent) -> None:
        """
        应用动态水印到页面元素
        """
        
        # 生成JavaScript代码注入到页面
        js_code = f"""
        (function() {{
            const element = document.getElementById('{element_id}');
            if (!element) return;
            
            const watermarkContainer = document.createElement('div');
            watermarkContainer.id = 'dynamic-watermark-{element_id}';
            watermarkContainer.style.cssText = `
                position: absolute;
                top: 0;
                left: 0;
                width: 100%;
                height: 100%;
                pointer-events: none;
                z-index: 9999;
                overflow: hidden;
            `;
            
            const watermarkDiv = document.createElement('div');
            watermarkDiv.style.cssText = `
                position: absolute;
                top: {random_position()}px;
                left: {random_position()}px;
                transform: rotate(-30deg);
                font-size: {watermark.size}px;
                color: rgba(128, 128, 128, {watermark.opacity});
                white-space: nowrap;
                opacity: {watermark.opacity};
            `;
            watermarkDiv.textContent = '{watermark.rendered}';
            
            watermarkContainer.appendChild(watermarkDiv);
            element.style.position = 'relative';
            element.appendChild(watermarkContainer);
            
            // 定时刷新
            setInterval(() => {{
                watermarkDiv.textContent = '{watermark.rendered}' + ' @' + new Date().toISOString();
            }}, {watermark.refresh_interval * 1000});
        }})();
        """
        
        return js_code
```

### 33.4 泄露溯源

#### 33.4.1 水印提取与溯源

```python
class WatermarkExtractor:
    """水印提取器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.parser_registry = WatermarkParserRegistry()
        self.token_verifier = TokenVerifier()
        self.evidence_collector = EvidenceCollector()
    
    def extract_watermark(self,
                         leaked_data: LeakedData) -> WatermarkExtractionResult:
        """
        从泄露数据中提取水印
        """
        
        # 1. 识别数据类型
        data_type = self.identify_data_type(leaked_data)
        
        # 2. 选择解析器
        parser = self.parser_registry.get_parser(data_type)
        
        # 3. 提取水印
        extracted = parser.extract(leaked_data)
        
        if not extracted:
            return WatermarkExtractionResult(
                status='not_found',
                message='未检测到水印'
            )
        
        # 4. 验证令牌
        verification = self.token_verifier.verify(extracted.token)
        
        if not verification.is_valid:
            return WatermarkExtractionResult(
                status='invalid_token',
                message='水印令牌无效',
                extracted_watermark=extracted
            )
        
        # 5. 收集证据
        evidence = self.evidence_collector.collect(
            watermark=extracted,
            verification=verification
        )
        
        return WatermarkExtractionResult(
            status='success',
            watermark=extracted,
            verification=verification,
            evidence=evidence,
            traced_user=self.get_user_by_id(extracted.user_id),
            traced_export=self.get_export_by_id(extracted.export_id)
        )
    
    def generate_investigation_report(self,
                                       extraction: WatermarkExtractionResult) -> InvestigationReport:
        """
        生成溯源调查报告
        """
        
        return InvestigationReport(
            report_id=self.generate_report_id(),
            generated_at=datetime.now(),
            watermark_info=WatermarkInfo(
                watermark_id=extraction.watermark.id,
                watermark_type=extraction.watermark.type,
                embedded_at=extraction.watermark.embedded_at
            ),
            traced_user=TracedUser(
                user_id=extraction.traced_user.id,
                user_name=extraction.traced_user.name,
                email=extraction.traced_user.email,
                department=extraction.traced_user.department,
                manager=extraction.traced_user.manager
            ),
            export_record=ExportRecord(
                export_id=extraction.traced_export.id,
                export_time=extraction.traced_export.export_time,
                export_method=extraction.traced_export.method,
                data_scope=extraction.traced_export.scope,
                approved_by=extraction.traced_export.approved_by
            ),
            evidence_summary=EvidenceSummary(
                chain_of_custody=extraction.evidence.custody_chain,
                digital_signature_valid=extraction.evidence.signature_valid,
                timestamp_verified=extraction.evidence.timestamp_verified
            ),
            conclusions=self.generate_conclusions(extraction),
            recommendations=self.generate_recommendations(extraction)
        )
```

## 第三十四章 数据质量SLA保障

### 34.1 功能定位

数据质量SLA保障模块建立数据质量的服务级别承诺和保障机制，明确数据提供方对数据消费者的质量承诺。

核心目标：
1. **承诺明确**：为不同级别的数据资产定义质量服务级别承诺
2. **实时监控**：监控各数据资产的质量指标与SLA承诺的差距
3. **及时告警**：当数据质量指标低于SLA承诺时自动告警
4. **责任追溯**：定期生成SLA达成报告，支持合规审计

### 34.2 SLA定义

#### 34.2.1 SLA管理框架

```python
class QualitySlaManager:
    """质量SLA管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.sla_repository = SlaRepository()
        self.metric_collector = MetricCollector()
        self.compliance_checker = ComplianceChecker()
    
    def define_sla(self, sla_def: SlaDefinition) -> QualitySla:
        """
        定义质量SLA
        """
        
        # 1. 验证SLA定义
        validation = self.validate_sla_definition(sla_def)
        if not validation.is_valid:
            raise InvalidSlaError(validation.errors)
        
        # 2. 创建SLA
        sla = QualitySla(
            id=self.generate_sla_id(),
            name=sla_def.name,
            description=sla_def.description,
            asset_scope=sla_def.asset_scope,
            tier=sla_def.tier,  # bronze, silver, gold, platinum
            commitments=CommitmentSet(
                freshness=SlaCommitment(
                    metric='update_frequency',
                    target=sla_def.commitments.freshness.target,
                    unit=sla_def.commitments.freshness.unit,
                    tolerance=sla_def.commitments.freshness.tolerance
                ),
                accuracy=SlaCommitment(
                    metric='data_accuracy',
                    target=sla_def.commitments.accuracy.target,
                    unit='percentage',
                    tolerance=sla_def.commitments.accuracy.tolerance
                ),
                completeness=SlaCommitment(
                    metric='data_completeness',
                    target=sla_def.commitments.completeness.target,
                    unit='percentage',
                    tolerance=sla_def.commitments.completeness.tolerance
                ),
                availability=SlaCommitment(
                    metric='service_availability',
                    target=sla_def.commitments.availability.target,
                    unit='percentage',
                    tolerance=sla_def.commitments.availability.tolerance
                )
            ),
            escalation_rules=sla_def.escalation_rules,
            created_by=sla_def.creator,
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            status='draft'
        )
        
        return self.sla_repository.save(sla)
    
    def activate_sla(self, sla_id: str) -> QualitySla:
        """
        激活SLA
        """
        
        sla = self.sla_repository.get(sla_id)
        
        # 验证SLA完整性
        completeness = self.check_sla_completeness(sla)
        if not completeness.is_complete:
            raise IncompleteSlaError(completeness.missing_parts)
        
        # 关联SLA到范围内的资产
        assets = self.asset_scanner.scan(sla.asset_scope)
        for asset in assets:
            self.link_sla_to_asset(sla_id, asset.id)
        
        sla.status = 'active'
        sla.activated_at = datetime.now()
        
        return self.sla_repository.save(sla)
```

### 34.3 SLA监控

#### 34.3.1 实时监控机制

```python
class SlaComplianceMonitor:
    """SLA合规监控器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.metric_store = MetricTimeSeriesStore()
        self.threshold_manager = ThresholdManager()
        self.alert_manager = AlertManager()
    
    def check_compliance(self, 
                        sla_id: str,
                        check_time: datetime = None) -> ComplianceCheckResult:
        """
        检查SLA合规状态
        """
        
        check_time = check_time or datetime.now()
        sla = self.sla_repository.get(sla_id)
        
        # 收集各指标数据
        metrics = {}
        for commitment_name, commitment in sla.commitments.items():
            metric_data = self.collect_metric(
                sla_id=sla_id,
                metric_name=commitment.metric,
                time_range=self.get_time_range(commitment, check_time)
            )
            metrics[commitment_name] = metric_data
        
        # 计算合规状态
        compliance_results = {}
        overall_compliance = True
        
        for name, commitment in sla.commitments.items():
            result = self.evaluate_commitment(
                commitment=commitment,
                actual_value=metrics[name].current_value,
                historical_values=metrics[name].historical_values
            )
            compliance_results[name] = result
            if not result.is_compliant:
                overall_compliance = False
        
        return ComplianceCheckResult(
            sla_id=sla_id,
            check_time=check_time,
            overall_compliant=overall_compliance,
            commitments=compliance_results,
            risk_level=self.assess_risk_level(compliance_results)
        )
    
    def monitor_loop(self, interval_seconds: int = 60) -> None:
        """
        持续监控循环
        """
        
        while True:
            # 获取所有活跃SLA
            active_slas = self.sla_repository.get_active_slas()
            
            for sla in active_slas:
                # 检查合规状态
                check_result = self.check_compliance(sla.id)
                
                # 记录检查结果
                self.record_compliance_check(check_result)
                
                # 处理违规情况
                if not check_result.overall_compliant:
                    self.handle_non_compliance(sla, check_result)
            
            time.sleep(interval_seconds)
    
    def handle_non_compliance(self,
                             sla: QualitySla,
                             check_result: ComplianceCheckResult) -> None:
        """
        处理SLA不合规情况
        """
        
        # 1. 检查是否已触发告警
        recent_alerts = self.alert_manager.get_recent_alerts(
            sla_id=sla.id,
            time_window=timedelta(hours=1)
        )
        
        if recent_alerts:
            return  # 避免重复告警
        
        # 2. 确定告警级别
        alert_level = self.determine_alert_level(check_result)
        
        # 3. 创建告警
        alert = self.create_alert(
            sla_id=sla.id,
            alert_level=alert_level,
            violations=check_result.get_violations(),
            affected_assets=self.get_affected_assets(sla.id)
        )
        
        # 4. 触发升级流程
        if alert_level == 'critical':
            self.trigger_escalation(sla, alert)
        
        # 5. 通知责任人
        self.notify_stakeholders(sla, alert)
```

### 34.4 SLA告警

#### 34.4.1 告警规则配置

```python
class SlaAlertRule:
    """SLA告警规则"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.rule_engine = AlertRuleEngine()
        self.notification_router = NotificationRouter()
    
    def create_alert_rule(self,
                         rule_def: AlertRuleDefinition) -> AlertRule:
        """
        创建告警规则
        """
        
        rule = AlertRule(
            id=self.generate_rule_id(),
            name=rule_def.name,
            sla_tier=rule_def.sla_tier,  # 匹配的SLA等级
            conditions=rule_def.conditions,
            severity_mapping=rule_def.severity_mapping,
            notification_targets=rule_def.notification_targets,
            auto_remediation=rule_def.auto_remediation,
            enabled=True,
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        
        return self.rule_engine.save(rule)
    
    def evaluate_rule(self, 
                     rule: AlertRule,
                     compliance_result: ComplianceCheckResult) -> Alert:
        """
        评估告警规则
        """
        
        # 1. 检查是否适用
        if not self.is_applicable(rule, compliance_result):
            return None
        
        # 2. 评估条件
        condition_results = []
        for condition in rule.conditions:
            result = self.evaluate_condition(condition, compliance_result)
            condition_results.append(result)
        
        # 3. 确定告警级别
        severity = self.determine_severity(
            rule.severity_mapping,
            condition_results
        )
        
        if severity:
            return Alert(
                id=self.generate_alert_id(),
                rule_id=rule.id,
                sla_id=compliance_result.sla_id,
                severity=severity,
                triggered_conditions=condition_results,
                created_at=datetime.now(),
                status='triggered'
            )
        
        return None
```

### 34.5 SLA报告

#### 34.5.1 报告生成

```python
class SlaReportGenerator:
    """SLA报告生成器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.report_repository = ReportRepository()
        self.chart_generator = ChartGenerator()
        self.template_engine = ReportTemplateEngine()
    
    def generate_sla_report(self,
                            period: ReportPeriod,
                            scope: ReportScope) -> SlaReport:
        """
        生成SLA报告
        """
        
        # 1. 收集期间数据
        sla_statuses = self.collect_period_data(period, scope)
        
        # 2. 计算统计指标
        statistics = self.calculate_statistics(sla_statuses)
        
        # 3. 生成趋势图表
        trend_charts = self.generate_trend_charts(
            sla_statuses,
            period
        )
        
        # 4. 生成详细分析
        analysis = self.generate_analysis(sla_statuses)
        
        # 5. 生成改进建议
        recommendations = self.generate_recommendations(
            sla_statuses,
            statistics
        )
        
        report = SlaReport(
            id=self.generate_report_id(),
            title=f"{period.start_date} 至 {period.end_date} 数据质量SLA报告",
            period=period,
            scope=scope,
            executive_summary=self.generate_executive_summary(statistics),
            overall_compliance_rate=statistics.compliance_rate,
            sla_tier_breakdown=statistics.by_tier,
            trend_analysis=trend_charts,
            detailed_analysis=analysis,
            recommendations=recommendations,
            generated_at=datetime.now(),
            generated_by='system'
        )
        
        return self.report_repository.save(report)
    
    def generate_executive_summary(self,
                                  statistics: SlaStatistics) -> ExecutiveSummary:
        """
        生成执行摘要
        """
        
        return ExecutiveSummary(
            compliance_status='达标' if statistics.compliance_rate >= 95 else '待改进',
            overall_compliance_rate=f"{statistics.compliance_rate:.1f}%",
            total_slas=statistics.total_slas,
            compliant_slas=statistics.compliant_slas,
            breached_slas=statistics.breached_slas,
            key_issues=[
                f" {item.commitment}: {item.breach_count}次违约" 
                for item in statistics.top_issues
            ],
            improvement_trend=statistics.trend,
            next_review_date=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=30)
        )
```

## 第三十五章 数据资产热度分析

### 35.1 功能定位

数据资产热度分析模块提供数据资产的使用热度分析和优化建议，帮助企业识别热点数据和冷数据，优化数据存储和访问策略。

核心目标：
1. **热度排行**：识别最受欢迎和最少使用的数据资产
2. **趋势预测**：分析使用趋势变化，预测未来需求
3. **优化建议**：基于热度分析提供存储优化建议
4. **成本控制**：优化存储成本，将冷数据迁移到低コスト存储

### 35.2 使用热度排行

#### 35.2.1 热度计算模型

```python
class AssetHeatAnalyzer:
    """资产热度分析器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.usage_collector = UsageDataCollector()
        self.heat_calculator = HeatCalculator()
        self.ranking_engine = RankingEngine()
    
    def calculate_heat_score(self,
                            asset_id: str,
                            time_range: TimeRange) -> HeatScore:
        """
        计算资产热度评分
        """
        
        # 1. 收集使用数据
        usage_data = self.usage_collector.collect(
            asset_id=asset_id,
            time_range=time_range
        )
        
        # 2. 计算各维度热度
        query_heat = self.heat_calculator.calculate_query_heat(
            queries=usage_data.queries,
            time_decay=True
        )
        
        access_heat = self.heat_calculator.calculate_access_heat(
            accesses=usage_data.accesses,
            time_decay=True
        )
        
        download_heat = self.heat_calculator.calculate_download_heat(
            downloads=usage_data.downloads,
            weight=3  # 下载权重更高
        )
        
        api_heat = self.heat_calculator.calculate_api_heat(
            api_calls=usage_data.api_calls,
            time_decay=True
        )
        
        # 3. 综合评分
        total_score = (
            query_heat * 0.3 +
            access_heat * 0.2 +
            download_heat * 0.3 +
            api_heat * 0.2
        )
        
        return HeatScore(
            asset_id=asset_id,
            time_range=time_range,
            total_score=total_score,
            breakdown=HeatBreakdown(
                query=query_heat,
                access=access_heat,
                download=download_heat,
                api=api_heat
            ),
            percentile=self.calculate_percentile(asset_id, total_score),
            calculated_at=datetime.now()
        )
    
    def get_heat_ranking(self,
                        time_range: TimeRange,
                        top_n: int = 100,
                        asset_type: str = None) -> HeatRanking:
        """
        获取热度排行榜
        """
        
        # 1. 获取所有资产的热度评分
        all_scores = self.get_all_heat_scores(time_range, asset_type)
        
        # 2. 排序
        sorted_scores = sorted(
            all_scores,
            key=lambda s: s.total_score,
            reverse=True
        )
        
        # 3. 获取Top N和Bottom N
        hot_assets = sorted_scores[:top_n]
        cold_assets = sorted_scores[-top_n:][::-1]
        
        return HeatRanking(
            time_range=time_range,
            hot_assets=hot_assets,
            cold_assets=cold_assets,
            total_analyzed=len(sorted_scores),
            generated_at=datetime.now()
        )
```

### 35.3 访问趋势分析

#### 35.3.1 趋势预测模型

```python
class UsageTrendAnalyzer:
    """使用趋势分析器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.time_series_store = TimeSeriesStore()
        self.forecasting_model = TrendForecastingModel()
        self.pattern_detector = PatternDetector()
    
    def analyze_trend(self,
                     asset_id: str,
                     analysis_period: TimeRange) -> TrendAnalysis:
        """
        分析使用趋势
        """
        
        # 1. 获取历史数据
        historical_data = self.time_series_store.get(
            metric='asset_access',
            asset_id=asset_id,
            time_range=analysis_period
        )
        
        # 2. 检测趋势模式
        patterns = self.pattern_detector.detect(historical_data)
        
        # 3. 预测未来趋势
        forecast = self.forecasting_model.predict(
            historical_data=historical_data,
            forecast_period=timedelta(days=30)
        )
        
        # 4. 识别异常
        anomalies = self.detect_anomalies(historical_data)
        
        # 5. 计算趋势指标
        indicators = self.calculate_trend_indicators(historical_data)
        
        return TrendAnalysis(
            asset_id=asset_id,
            analysis_period=analysis_period,
            current_trend=indicators.trend_direction,  # 'increasing', 'stable', 'decreasing'
            growth_rate=indicators.growth_rate,
            seasonality=patterns.seasonality,
            forecast=forecast,
            anomalies=anomalies,
            confidence_level=forecast.confidence
        )
    
    def identify_rising_assets(self,
                               period: TimeRange) -> List[RisingAsset]:
        """
        识别上升潜力的资产
        """
        
        # 1. 计算各资产的增长率
        assets = self.get_all_active_assets()
        rising_candidates = []
        
        for asset in assets:
            trend = self.analyze_trend(asset.id, period)
            
            # 筛选上升趋势明显的资产
            if trend.growth_rate > 0.2 and trend.current_trend == 'increasing':
                rising_candidates.append(RisingAsset(
                    asset_id=asset.id,
                    asset_name=asset.name,
                    growth_rate=trend.growth_rate,
                    current_usage=trend.current_usage_level,
                    predicted_future_rank=trend.forecast.future_rank
                ))
        
        return sorted(
            rising_candidates,
            key=lambda a: a.growth_rate,
            reverse=True
        )
```

### 35.4 优化建议

#### 35.4.1 存储优化推荐

```python
class StorageOptimizationAdvisor:
    """存储优化顾问"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.tier_manager = StorageTierManager()
        self.cost_calculator = CostCalculator()
        self.migration_planner = MigrationPlanner()
    
    def generate_optimization_suggestions(self,
                                          heat_analysis: HeatRanking) -> OptimizationSuggestions:
        """
        生成优化建议
        """
        
        suggestions = []
        
        # 1. 识别可归档的冷数据
        cold_data_suggestions = self.suggest_cold_data_archive(
            heat_analysis.cold_assets
        )
        suggestions.extend(cold_data_suggestions)
        
        # 2. 识别需要升级存储的热点数据
        hot_upgrade_suggestions = self.suggest_hot_data_upgrade(
            heat_analysis.hot_assets
        )
        suggestions.extend(hot_upgrade_suggestions)
        
        # 3. 识别需要清理的孤儿数据
        orphan_suggestions = self.suggest_orphan_cleanup()
        suggestions.extend(orphan_suggestions)
        
        # 4. 计算优化收益
        benefits = self.calculate_optimization_benefits(suggestions)
        
        return OptimizationSuggestions(
            suggestions=suggestions,
            estimated_savings=benefits.total_savings,
            storage_reduction=benefits.storage_reduction,
            priority_order=self.prioritize_suggestions(suggestions)
        )
    
    def suggest_cold_data_archive(self,
                                  cold_assets: List[HeatScore]) -> List[OptimizationSuggestion]:
        """
        建议冷数据归档
        """
        
        suggestions = []
        
        for asset in cold_assets:
            # 检查是否符合归档条件
            if self.meets_archive_criteria(asset):
                cost_current = self.cost_calculator.calculate_cost(
                    asset.storage_tier,
                    asset.storage_size
                )
                cost_archive = self.cost_calculator.calculate_cost(
                    'archive_tier',
                    asset.storage_size
                )
                
                savings = cost_current - cost_archive
                
                suggestions.append(OptimizationSuggestion(
                    suggestion_id=self.generate_suggestion_id(),
                    type='archive',
                    asset_id=asset.asset_id,
                    asset_name=asset.asset_name,
                    reason=f"连续{asset.inactive_days}天无访问",
                    action='迁移到归档存储',
                    current_tier=asset.storage_tier,
                    recommended_tier='archive_tier',
                    estimated_savings_monthly=savings,
                    risk_level='low',
                    rollback_available=True
                ))
        
        return suggestions
    
    def calculate_optimization_benefits(self,
                                        suggestions: List[OptimizationSuggestion]) -> OptimizationBenefits:
        """
        计算优化收益
        """
        
        total_savings = sum(s.estimated_savings_monthly for s in suggestions)
        storage_reduction = sum(
            self.get_asset_size(s.asset_id) for s in suggestions 
            if s.type in ['archive', 'delete']
        )
        
        return OptimizationBenefits(
            total_savings=total_savings,
            monthly_savings=total_savings,
            yearly_savings=total_savings * 12,
            storage_reduction_gb=storage_reduction,
            affected_assets=len(suggestions)
        )
```

## 第三十六章 多语言与国际化支持

### 36.1 功能定位

多语言与国际化模块支持系统界面的多语言切换，满足国际化企业需求。该模块支持中文、英文、日文、韩文等多种语言界面，并提供语言包的在线管理和自定义翻译功能。

核心目标：
1. **界面国际化**：支持多语言界面切换
2. **语言包管理**：提供语言包在线编辑和批量导入功能
3. **数据翻译**：支持业务术语、数据字典的多语言翻译
4. **格式适配**：支持不同地区的时间、数字、货币格式

### 36.2 多语言界面

#### 36.2.1 国际化框架

```python
class InternationalizationService:
    """国际化服务"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.locale_detector = LocaleDetector()
        self.translation_provider = TranslationProvider()
        self.format_adapter = FormatAdapter()
    
    def get_user_locale(self, user_id: str) -> Locale:
        """
        获取用户语言偏好
        """
        
        # 1. 获取用户设置
        user_setting = self.user_settings.get(user_id)
        if user_setting and user_setting.preferred_locale:
            return Locale.from_code(user_setting.preferred_locale)
        
        # 2. 获取浏览器语言
        browser_locale = self.locale_detector.get_browser_locale()
        if browser_locale and self.is_supported(browser_locale):
            return browser_locale
        
        # 3. 返回默认语言
        return Locale.from_code('zh-CN')
    
    def translate(self,
                 key: str,
                 locale: Locale,
                 params: dict = None) -> str:
        """
        获取翻译文本
        """
        
        # 1. 获取翻译
        translation = self.translation_provider.get(
            key=key,
            locale=locale
        )
        
        if not translation:
            # 回退到默认语言
            translation = self.translation_provider.get(
                key=key,
                locale=self.default_locale
            )
            
            if not translation:
                return key  # 返回原始key
        
        # 2. 替换参数
        if params:
            translation = self.interpolate_params(translation, params)
        
        return translation
    
    def format_date(self,
                   date: datetime,
                   locale: Locale,
                   format_type: str = 'default') -> str:
        """
        格式化日期
        """
        
        return self.format_adapter.format_date(
            date=date,
            locale=locale,
            format_type=format_type
        )
    
    def format_number(self,
                     number: float,
                     locale: Locale,
                     options: NumberFormatOptions = None) -> str:
        """
        格式化数字
        """
        
        return self.format_adapter.format_number(
            number=number,
            locale=locale,
            options=options
        )
```

### 36.3 语言包管理

#### 36.3.1 语言包编辑

```python
class LanguagePackManager:
    """语言包管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.pack_repository = LanguagePackRepository()
        self.editor = LanguagePackEditor()
        self.validator = TranslationValidator()
        self.importer = BatchImporter()
    
    def create_language_pack(self,
                            locale: Locale,
                            base_locale: Locale = None) -> LanguagePack:
        """
        创建语言包
        """
        
        # 1. 验证语言代码
        if not self.is_valid_locale(locale):
            raise InvalidLocaleError(locale)
        
        # 2. 从基础语言包复制（如指定）
        translations = {}
        if base_locale:
            base_pack = self.pack_repository.get(base_locale)
            if base_pack:
                translations = base_pack.translations.copy()
        
        # 3. 创建语言包
        pack = LanguagePack(
            id=self.generate_pack_id(),
            locale=locale,
            name=self.get_locale_name(locale),
            translations=translations,
            completeness=self.calculate_completeness(translations),
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            status='draft'
        )
        
        return self.pack_repository.save(pack)
    
    def update_translation(self,
                          pack_id: str,
                          key: str,
                          value: str,
                          updated_by: str) -> LanguagePack:
        """
        更新翻译
        """
        
        # 1. 验证翻译质量
        validation = self.validator.validate(key, value)
        if not validation.is_valid:
            raise InvalidTranslationError(validation.errors)
        
        # 2. 更新翻译
        pack = self.pack_repository.get(pack_id)
        pack.translations[key] = value
        pack.updated_at = datetime.now()
        pack.updated_by = updated_by
        pack.completeness = self.calculate_completeness(pack.translations)
        
        return self.pack_repository.save(pack)
    
    def batch_import(self,
                    pack_id: str,
                    file_content: bytes,
                    file_format: str,
                    imported_by: str) -> ImportResult:
        """
        批量导入翻译
        """
        
        # 1. 解析文件
        translations = self.importer.parse(
            content=file_content,
            format=file_format
        )
        
        # 2. 验证翻译
        validation_results = []
        valid_translations = {}
        
        for key, value in translations.items():
            validation = self.validator.validate(key, value)
            validation_results.append(validation)
            if validation.is_valid:
                valid_translations[key] = value
        
        # 3. 更新语言包
        pack = self.pack_repository.get(pack_id)
        pack.translations.update(valid_translations)
        pack.updated_at = datetime.now()
        pack.updated_by = imported_by
        self.pack_repository.save(pack)
        
        return ImportResult(
            total=len(translations),
            success=len(valid_translations),
            failed=len(translations) - len(valid_translations),
            validation_results=validation_results
        )
```

### 36.4 数据翻译

#### 36.4.1 业务术语翻译

```python
class DataTranslationService:
    """数据翻译服务"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.translation_cache = TranslationCache()
        self.term_repository = TermRepository()
        self.ml_translator = MLTranslator()
    
    def translate_term(self,
                      term: str,
                      source_locale: Locale,
                      target_locale: Locale,
                      context: dict = None) -> TranslatedTerm:
        """
        翻译业务术语
        """
        
        # 1. 检查缓存
        cached = self.translation_cache.get(term, source_locale, target_locale)
        if cached:
            return cached
        
        # 2. 查询术语库
        term_translation = self.term_repository.find_translation(
            term=term,
            source_locale=source_locale,
            target_locale=target_locale
        )
        
        if term_translation:
            result = TranslatedTerm(
                original=term,
                translation=term_translation.value,
                source_locale=source_locale,
                target_locale=target_locale,
                confidence=1.0,  # 术语库匹配为最高置信度
                source='terminology'
            )
        else:
            # 使用机器翻译
            result = self.ml_translator.translate(
                term=term,
                source_locale=source_locale,
                target_locale=target_locale,
                context=context
            )
            result.source = 'ml_translation'
        
        # 3. 缓存结果
        self.translation_cache.set(term, source_locale, target_locale, result)
        
        return result
    
    def translate_asset_metadata(self,
                                asset_id: str,
                                target_locale: Locale) -> TranslatedMetadata:
        """
        翻译资产元数据
        """
        
        asset = self.asset_repository.get(asset_id)
        
        return TranslatedMetadata(
            asset_id=asset_id,
            name=asset.name,
            translated_name=asset.translations.get(target_locale.code, {}).get('name'),
            description=asset.description,
            translated_description=asset.translations.get(target_locale.code, {}).get('description'),
            fields=[
                TranslatedField(
                    name=f.name,
                    translated_name=f.translations.get(target_locale.code, {}).get('name'),
                    comment=f.comment,
                    translated_comment=f.translations.get(target_locale.code, {}).get('comment')
                )
                for f in asset.fields
            ],
            target_locale=target_locale
        )
```
